< Review>
Came in on a Tuesday afternoon on my lunch break. Alex and whom I presumed to be his wife were each cutting someone else's hair. I was promptly greeted. My wait was approximately 15minutes. They do not take appointments, but from what I could tell they are both speedy, pay close attention to detail and are very good at what they do.

When I was due up, I told them that I needed to put some money in the meter as I was in the 24minute spot (street parking in front, downtown street parking nearby, also garage parking nearby). Alex himself offered me quarters. A+ for customer service. I declined as I had some, but they were very nice.

Additionally, I didn't exactly know how I wanted my hair cut as this was for a special event (Vegas 30th birthday). They gave me a fade and comb over which came out to $27 ($23 for a normal cut eg no fade). There is a $2 surcharge to use your card, but I didn't mind. This shop is very "mom and pop".

Overall, my haircut is great, we had a great conversation, they were very friendly and made me actually want to come back. My first experience here....5 stars. Thank you both!!!< /Review>

<rate>5<//rate>< review>
Have been here a number of times now and I just feel it gets better every time I go. Today was no exception. The clean look in the store makes it nice to come to also the wonderful smells coming from the kitchen. They were just cleaning up with the lunch buffet which happens Monday thru Friday from 11am to 2 pm. The staff member came over with a friendly attitude and took our order. We started our order with and order of garlic sticks with cheese. There is 12 nice size pieces with a nice garlic flavor and not overly cheesy and came with a nice cup of the pizza sauce to dip them in (actually the cup of pizza sauce came with at least two cups). We then added two large pizzas, the first was the specialty pizza called Pike's Peak. This is an all meat combination loaded with mounds of pepperoni, sausage, beef, salami, lingucia and ham. The second pizza consisted of pepperoni, ham and mushrooms. Both pizzas we're loaded with a load of toppings. The pizzas were very tasty and filling they are never worried about you going home hungry and usually you go home with leftovers which our just as good the next day.  The slices are a nice size and you can see the pleasure they put into each pizza. If you looking for good pizza this is definitely a great place to go and enjoy the atmosphere and great food you can't miss out.</review>

<rate>4</rate><review>This is a very nice and local spot to get some tasty Mexican food. Came here for the time and was pleasantly surprised.  My co-worker raved about this place.  But I keep my expectations within in reason as I didn't have a true sense of my coworkers palette.

I got the combination taco and enchilada plate, my sister the garlic shrimp and our friend the carnitas plate along with a michilada. The meat in the taco was tasty and juicy I really enjoyed it. The garlic shrimp was perfectly garlicky and the carnitas were abundant and nice big chunks. I'm not a michilada kind of person but this one was actually good.

I would totally recommend this place. The service was very friendly and quick. The pricing is right and portions are too.  I would definitely come back and introduce it to others.</review>< pictures>

<review>This is a very nice and local spot to get some tasty Mexican food. Came here for the time and was pleasantly surprised.  My co-worker raved about this place.  But I keep my expectations within in reason as I didn't have a true sense of my coworkers palette.

I got the combination taco and enchilada plate, my sister the garlic shrimp and our friend the carnitas plate along with a michilada. The meat in the taco was tasty and juicy I really enjoyed it. The garlic shrimp was perfectly garlicky and the carnitas were abundant and nice big chunks. I'm not a michilada kind of person but this one was actually good.

I would totally recommend this place. The service was very friendly and quick. The pricing is right and portions are too.  I would definitely come back and introduce it to others.<//review>< Response>

First time maybe last. Seems they charge for everything. Asked for an extra small bag of chips since I seen other pick up orders with two bags, hostess charged me $1.50. $1.00 fee if order is under $10 bucks. Ordered 2 No. #56 Shredded Beef burritos, was not impressed. Salsa over the burrito was not that great but I must say the beef tamale was excellent. Prices are a bit too much for some items I saw on the menu. Overall it wasn't what my wife and I expected. I chose to come here after reading some of the good reviews but after eating here today I think those reviews were a bit exaggerating.</text>

Anyway, long story short he began yelling at us... The customer and saying anywhere you go you have to pay for extra things you order. I was so upset.
